<script>
function setAikidoHsCookies(){
  var relevantUtmParams = [
    "utm_source",
    "utm_medium",
    "utm_campaign",
    "utm_adgroup",
    "utm_term",
    "matchtype",
    "device",
    "utm_content",
    "gclid",
    "msclkid",
    "li_fat_id",
    "fbclid",
    "partner",
    "rdt_cid"
  ];
  var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
  for(var i = 0; i < relevantUtmParams.length; i++)
  {
    var paramValue = urlParams.get(relevantUtmParams[i]);
    // expires in 60 days
    var expires = new Date(Date.now() + 60 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
    expires = expires.toUTCString();
    if(paramValue){
      document.cookie = relevantUtmParams[i]+"="+paramValue+"; path=/; secure; expires="+expires+"; domain=.aikido.dev";
    }
  }
}
// let's wait a few seconds
setTimeout(setAikidoHsCookies, 500);

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
        var navbar = document.querySelector('.navbar_wrap');
        if (window.innerWidth > 991) { // Check if screen width is greater than 991 pixels
            if (window.scrollY > 100) { // Change to use 100 pixels
                navbar.classList.add('is--open'); // Add class to navbar
            } else {
                navbar.classList.remove('is--open'); // Remove class from navbar
            }
        } else {
            navbar.classList.remove('is--open'); // Ensure the class is removed on smaller screens
        }
    });
});

document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
    const dropdownToggles = document.querySelectorAll('.navbar_dropdown_toggle');
		const menu = document.querySelector(".navbar_menu_wrapper")

    dropdownToggles.forEach(toggle => {
        toggle.addEventListener('click', function() {
            // Check if the screen width is 991 pixels or below
            if (window.innerWidth <= 991) {
                const parent = this.parentElement;
                // Log the correct parent element
                console.log(this, parent);

                menu.scrollTo({
                    top: parent.getBoundingClientRect().top + menu.scrollY,
                    behavior: 'smooth' // Smooth scroll
                });
            }
        });
    });
});

pricing models. Tools that will overload you with irrelevant alerts and false positives.</p><div class="padding-small padding-bottom"></div><img loading="lazy" class="container-large"><div class="features_text"><img loading="lazy" src="https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/642adcaf364024552e71df01/642adcaf364024a62571df4f_Down.svg" alt="down arrow" class="features_arrow"/><div class="padding-small padding-bottom"></div><h2 class="heading-style-h4">We&#x27;ll take the sifting off your hands and notify you when it matters.</h2></div></div><div class="padding-bottom padding-large"></div></div><div class="line-divider"></div><div class="padding-global"><div class="container-large"><div class="padding-bottom padding-large"></div><div class="w-layout-grid features_list_triage"><div class="features_item"><div class="margin-bottom margin-custom1"><img loading="lazy" class="heading-style-h6 is-alt-text">Deduplication</h3></div><p class="text-color-grey-light">Groups related issues so you can quickly solve as many issues as possible.</p></div><div class="features_item"><div class="margin-bottom margin-custom1"><img loading="lazy" src="https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/642adcaf364024552e71df01/642adcaf364024cd0971df98_traige-diamond.svg" alt="" class="icon-1x1-large"/></div><div class="margin-bottom margin-xxsmall"><h3 class="heading-style-h6 is-alt-text">AutoTriage</h3></div><p class="text-color-grey-light">Analyzes &amp; monitors your codebase and infrastructure to automatically filter out issues that don’t affect you.</p></div><div class="features_item"><div class="margin-bottom margin-custom1"><img loading="lazy" src="https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/642adcaf364024552e71df01/642adcaf3640246b5171dfb8_eye.svg" alt="" class="icon-1x1-large"/></div><div class="margin-bottom margin-xxsmall"><h3 class="heading-style-h6">Custom Rules</h3></div><p class="text-color-grey-light">Set up custom rules to filter out the irrelevant paths, packages etc. You’ll still get alerted when there’s a critical issue.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="padding-bottom padding-large"></div><div class="padding-global"><div class="container-large"><div class="features_text"><img loading="lazy" src="https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/642adcaf364024552e71df01/642adcaf364024a62571df4f_Down.svg" alt="down arrow" class="features_arrow"/><div class="padding-small padding-bottom"></div><h2 class="heading-style-h4">We&#x27;ll give you the tools you need to fix issues.</h2></div></div><div class="padding-bottom padding-large"></div></div><div class="line-divider"></div><div class="icon-1x1-large"/></div><h3 class="heading-style-h6 is-alt-text">AutoFix</h3></div><p class="text-color-grey-light">Fix issues with Aikido&#x27;s AI agent. Generate pull requests to fix SAST, IaC, dependency, and container issues - or switch to hardened base images.<br/></p></div><div class="features_item"><div class="margin-bottom margin-xxsmall"><div class="margin-bottom margin-custom1"><img loading="lazy" src="https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/642adcaf364024552e71df01/678dff76aabf9b67d64a71db_bulk.svg" alt="" class="icon-1x1-large"/></div><h3 class="heading-style-h6 is-alt-text">Bulk Fix with One Click</h3></div><p class="text-color-grey-light">Create ready to merge PRs to solve multiple issues at once. Save hours of development time and ticketing work.</p></div><div class="features_item"><div class="margin-bottom margin-xxsmall"><div class="margin-bottom margin-custom1"><img loading="lazy" src="https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/642adcaf364024552e71df01/677d4ba246ad7d8c4a1c4679_Icon%20aiai.svg" alt="" class="icon-1x1-large"/></div><h3 class="heading-style-h6">TL;DR Summaries</h3></div><p class="text-color-grey-light">For more complex issues, get a short summary of the issue and how to fix it. Create a ticket and assign it in one click</p></div></div></div></div></div></section><section class="section_home_trust"><div class="padding-global"><div class="container-large"><div class="padding-section-large"><div class="home_trust_component"><div class="home_trust_content-left"><div class="tag is-disabled display-inlineflex">Trust</div><div class="padding-bottom padding-medium"></div><h2 class="heading-style-h3">Taking care of your data like it’s our own</h2><div class="home_trust_nav-wrapper is-top-margin"><div class="text-color-purple text-weight-semibold text-size-tiny">More to explore</div><div class="padding-bottom padding-small"></div><div class="home_trust_nav-list"><a href="https://help.aikido.dev/doc/overview-aikido-docs/docCpLHBMatZ" target="_blank" class="home_trust_nav-link w-inline-block"><div class="home_trust_nav-link-text">Documentation</div><div class="home_trust_nav-icon w-embed"><svg width="100%" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">

<path d="M8 13.3333L10.7692 16L17 10" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="square" stroke-linejoin="round"/>
</svg></div><h3 class="heading-style-h6">How does Aikido know which alerts are relevant?</h3><div class="home_trust_open-icon w-embed"><svg width=" 100%" height=" 100%" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
<path d="M4 7.5L8 11.5L12 7.5" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="square" stroke-linejoin="round"/>
</svg></div></div><div class="home_trust_bottom"><div class="home_trust_bottom-inner is-pricing"><p>We’ve built a rule engine that takes the context of your environment into account. This allows us to easily adapt the criticality score for your environment &amp; filter out false positives. If we’re not sure, the algorithm always reverts to the safest option...</p></div></div></div></div><div role="listitem" class="w-dyn-item"><div class="home_trust_item"><div id="first-accordion" class="home_trust_top"><div class="home_trust_top-check-icon w-embed"><svg width=" 100%" height=" 100%" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
<path d="M8 13.3333L10.7692 16L17 10" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="square" stroke-linejoin="round"/>
</svg></div><h3 class="heading-style-h6">What happens to my data?</h3><div class="home_trust_open-icon w-embed"><svg width=" 100%" height=" 100%" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
<path d="M4 7.5L8 11.5L12 7.5" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="square" stroke-linejoin="round"/>
</svg></div></div><div class="home_trust_bottom"><div class="home_trust_bottom-inner is-pricing"><p>We clone the repositories inside of temporary environments (such as docker containers unique to you). Those containers are disposed of, after analysis. The duration of the test and scans themselves take about 1-5 mins. All the clones and containers are then auto-removed after that, always, every time, for every customer.</p></div></div></div></div><div role="listitem" class="w-dyn-item"><div class="home_trust_item"><div id="first-accordion" class="home_trust_top"><div class="home_trust_top-check-icon w-embed"><svg width=" 100%" height=" 100%" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
<path d="M8 13.3333L10.7692 16L17 10" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="square" stroke-linejoin="round"/>
</svg></div><h3 class="heading-style-h6">Does Aikido make changes to my codebase?</h3><div class="home_trust_open-icon w-embed"><svg width=" 100%" height=" 100%" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
<path d="M4 7.5L8 11.5L12 7.5" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="square" stroke-linejoin="round"/>
</svg></div></div><div class="home_trust_bottom"><div class="home_trust_bottom-inner is-pricing"><p>We can’t &amp; won’t, this is guaranteed by read-only access.</p></div></div></div></div><div role="listitem" class="w-dyn-item"><div class="home_trust_item"><div id="first-accordion" class="home_trust_top"><div class="home_trust_top-check-icon w-embed"><svg width=" 100%" height=" 100%" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
<path d="M8 13.3333L10.7692 16L17 10" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="square" stroke-linejoin="round"/>
</svg></div><h3 class="heading-style-h6">I don’t want to connect my repository. Can I try it with a test account?</h3><div class="home_trust_open-icon w-embed"><svg width=" 100%" height=" 100%" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
<path d="M4 7.5L8 11.5L12 7.5" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="square" stroke-linejoin="round"/>
</svg></div></div><div class="home_trust_bottom"><div class="home_trust_bottom-inner is-pricing"><p>Of course! When you sign up with your git, don’t give access to any repo &amp; select the demo repo instead!</p></div></div></div></div><div role="listitem" class="w-dyn-item"><div class="home_trust_item"><div id="first-accordion" class="home_trust_top"><div class="home_trust_top-check-icon w-embed"><svg width=" 100%" height=" 100%" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
<path d="M8 13.3333L10.7692 16L17 10" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="square" stroke-linejoin="round"/>
</svg></div><h3 class="heading-style-h6">How is Aikido different?</h3><div class="home_trust_open-icon w-embed"><svg width=" 100%" height=" 100%" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
<path d="M4 7.5L8 11.5L12 7.5" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="square" stroke-linejoin="round"/>
</svg></div></div><div class="home_trust_bottom"><div class="home_trust_bottom-inner is-pricing"><p>Aikido combines features from lots of different platforms in one. By bringing together multiple tools in one platform, we’re able to contextualize vulnerabilities, filter out false positives and reduce noise by 95%.</p></div></div></div></div><div role="listitem" class="w-dyn-item"><div class="home_trust_item"><div id="first-accordion" class="home_trust_top"><div class="home_trust_top-check-icon w-embed"><svg width=" 100%" height=" 100%" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">

</svg></div><h3 class="heading-style-h6">How can I trust Aikido?</h3><div class="home_trust_open-icon w-embed"><svg width=" 100%" height=" 100%" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
<path d="M4 7.5L8 11.5L12 7.5" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="square" stroke-linejoin="round"/>
</svg></div></div><div class="home_trust_bottom"><div class="home_trust_bottom-inner is-pricing"><p>We’re doing everything we can to be fully secure &amp; compliant. <script>
$(document).ready(function() {
  const emailRegex = /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/;

  function validateEmail(email) {
    return emailRegex.test(email);
  }
	$('div[email-error]').hide();
$('input[email-input]').on('input', function() {
  const email = $(this).val();
  if (validateEmail(email)) {
    $('div[email-error]').fadeOut(300); // Updated to fadeOut
  } else {
    $('div[email-error]').fadeIn(300); // Updated to fadeIn
  }
});

  $('form').on('submit', function(e) {
    if (!validateEmail($('input[email-input]').val())) {
      e.preventDefault();
    }
  });
});

</script>

<script>
  // Define your base URLs for each language, including PT
  const baseUrls = {
    en: "https://www.aikido.dev",
    fr: "https://fr.aikido.dev",
    ja: "https://jp.aikido.dev",
    de: "https://de.aikido.dev",
    pt: "https://pt.aikido.dev" // Portuguese version
  };

  // Get the current path from the URL
  const path = window.location.pathname;

  // Function to create hreflang tags
  function createHreflangTags() {
    let tags = '';
    for (const [lang, baseUrl] of Object.entries(baseUrls)) {
      const url = `${baseUrl}${path}`;
      tags += `<link rel="alternate" href="${url}" hreflang="${lang}" />\n`;
    }
    // Add the x-default tag
    const xDefault = `${baseUrls.en}${path}`;
    tags += `<link rel="alternate" href="${xDefault}" hreflang="x-default" />\n`;

    // Insert the tags into the head of the document
    const head = document.head || document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
    head.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', tags);
  }

  // Run the function to create and insert hreflang tags
  createHreflangTags();
</script>
